# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox DOM Event Dispatch Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a DOM event (e.g., click) is dispatched through the Firefox event system in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the event creation, the event target identification, the capture/bubble phase traversal, the event listener invocation, and the default action execution.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

## Summary

I've traced the complete Firefox DOM event dispatch system by analyzing the C++ source code in mozilla-firefox/gecko-dev. The analysis covers:

### Key Findings:

1. **Event Creation & Entry Point** - `EventTarget::DispatchEvent` (dom/events/EventTarget.cpp)
2. **Event Target Chain Construction** - `EventDispatcher::Dispatch` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869-1360)
3. **Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal** - `HandleEventTargetChain` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:480-694)
   - Capture phase: root → target
   - Target phase: at original target
   - Bubble phase: target → root
   - System event group for default actions

4. **Event Listener Invocation** - `EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1310)
   - Sets current target
   - Invokes individual listeners
   - Handles once, passive, and capture options

5. **Default Action Execution** - `ActivationBehavior` and `PostHandleEvent`
   - PreHandleEvent: Before listener invocation
   - PostHandleEvent: After listener invocation
   - ActivationBehavior: Default action (click, etc.)

The answer document includes file paths, line numbers, symbol references, and a detailed narrative explaining how the event dispatching chain works in Firefox's DOM implementation, with particular attention to the capture/bubble phase mechanics and event listener management.

following major components:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation and Entry Point\\n**EventTarget::DispatchEvent** (dom/events/EventTarget.cpp:212-222)\\n- Public API for dispatching events on any DOM element\\n- Overloaded versions accept Event references and ErrorResult\\n- Delegates to EventDispatcher::Dispatch for actual dispatching\\n\\n## 2. Event Listener Invocation\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1310)\\n- Invokes a single event listener on the current event target\\n- Steps:\\n  1. Compiles event handler if it's a string (lines 1261-1262)\\n  5. Calls listener.HandleEvent with EventTarget and Event (line 1276)\\n  6. Returns false if propagation stopped or immediate propagation stopped\\n\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventWithListenerArray** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1536-1627)\\n- Iterates through all listeners for an event type\\n- Filters by event phase (capture vs bubble)\\n- Handles 'once' listeners by removing them during dispatch\\n- Ensures DOM event is lazily created when first listener is invoked\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-375)\\n- Called for each item in the chain during appropriate phase\\n- Gets or creates EventListenerManager for the target\\n- Invokes EventListenerManager::HandleEvent to fire all listeners for this event type\\n\\n## 5. Event Flow Control\\n\\nThe dispatch process manages several flags in the event:\\n- mInCapturePhase: Currently in capture phase\\n- mInTargetPhase: Currently at the target\\n- mInBubblingPhase: Currently in bubble phase\\n- mPropagationStopped: stopPropagation() was called\\n- mImmediatePropagationStopped: stopImmediatePropagation() was called\\n- mDefaultPrevented: preventDefault() was called\\n\\nListeners can be configured as:\\n- Capturing (capture=true) - fires in capture phase\\n- Bubbling (capture=false) - fires in bubble phase and target phase\\n- Passive - cannot call preventDefault()\\n- Once - automatically removed after first invocation\\n\\n## 7. Shadow DOM and Retargeting\\n\\nThe event system handles:\\n- Event retargeting across shadow boundaries (EventChainPreVisitor lines 137-140)\\n- Composed path calculation considering shadow trees\\n- Target adjustment based on shadow tree composition\\n- Anonymous content retargeting\\n\\n## 8. EventTarget::DispatchEvent \u2192 EventDispatcher::Dispatch (creates chain)\\n2. Build event target chain via GetEventTargetParent (up to document/window)\\n3. Call PreHandleEvent on all targets (setup phase)\\n4. HandleEventTargetChain iterates:\\n   - Capture phase: root \u2192 target, invoke capture listeners\\n   - Target phase: invoke all listeners on original target\\n   - Bubble phase: target \u2192 root, invoke bubble listeners\\n5. PostHandleEvent called after listeners (post-processing)\\n6. Default group dispatch completes\\n7. System group dispatch with same phases\\n8. ActivationBehavior executed if not prevented (default action)\\n\\nThis design separates concerns between event routing, listener management, and default action handling, allowing flexible event processing in Firefox's DOM implementation.\"\n}\n",

following major components:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation and Entry Point\\n**EventTarget::DispatchEvent** (dom/events/EventTarget.cpp:212-222)\\n- Public API for dispatching events on any DOM element\\n- Overloaded versions accept Event references and ErrorResult\\n- Delegates to EventDispatcher::Dispatch for actual dispatching\\n\\n## 2. Event Target Chain Construction\\n**EventDispatcher::Dispatch** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869-1360)\\n- Main event dispatching orchestrator\\n- Creates the event target chain by calling GetEventTargetParent on each target\\n- Initializes EventChainPreVisitor to track pre-dispatch state\\n- Builds chain upward from initial target through parents until no more parents exist\\n- Handles event retargeting for Shadow DOM and anonymous content\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h/cpp)\\n- Represents individual items in the event target chain\\n- Contains methods:\\n  - GetEventTargetParent: Builds chain by calling target's GetEventTargetParent method\\n  - PreHandleEvent: Called before event listener invocation\\n  - PostHandleEvent: Called after event listener invocation  \\n  - HandleEvent: Invokes event listeners via EventListenerManager\\n  - ActivationBehavior: Executes default actions\\n\\n## 3. Event Listener Invocation\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1310)\\n- Invokes a single event listener on the current event target\\n- Steps:\\n  1. Sets event.currentTarget to the current target (line 1237)\\n  2. Marks if listener is passive (line 1243)\\n  3. Stores previous window event for proper scoping\\n  4. Compiles event handler if it's a string (lines 1261-1262)\\n  5. Calls listener.HandleEvent with EventTarget and Event (line 1276)\\n  6. Returns false if propagation stopped or immediate propagation stopped\\n\\n**EventListenerManager::HandleEventWithListenerArray** (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1536-1627)\\n- Iterates through all listeners for an event type\\n- Filters by event phase (capture vs bubble)\\n- Handles 'once' listeners by removing them during dispatch\\n- Ensures DOM event is lazily created when first listener is invoked\\n\\n**EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-375)\\n- Called for each item in the chain during appropriate phase\\n- Gets or creates EventListenerManager for the target\\n- Invokes EventListenerManager::HandleEvent to fire all listeners for this event type\\n\\n## 5. Default Action Execution\\n\\n**PreHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:455-458)\\n- Called BEFORE event listeners are invoked\\n- Allows targets to perform preparatory actions\\n- Can set flags to influence listener invocation\\n- Called during the pre-dispatch phase (EventDispatcher::Dispatch lines 1077-1078, 1200)\\n\\n**PostHandleEvent** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-524)\\n- Called AFTER event listeners are invoked for each target\\n- Called only in system event group dispatch (lines 609, 645)\\n- Updates visitor with target's item flags and data\\n- Can modify event handling based on listener results\\n\\n**ActivationBehavior** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp)\\n- Executes default action for activation events (click, etc.)\\n- Called after event dispatch completes if:\\n  - Event wasn't preventDefault'd (line 1340)\\n  - Target was marked as activation target during dispatch\\n- Implementations in specific elements (HTMLButtonElement, HTMLInputElement, etc.)\\n\\n## 6. Event Flow Control\\n\\nThe dispatch process manages several flags in the event:\\n- mInCapturePhase: Currently in capture phase\\n- mInTargetPhase: Currently at the target\\n- mInBubblingPhase: Currently in bubble phase\\n- mPropagationStopped: stopPropagation() was called\\n- mImmediatePropagationStopped: stopImmediatePropagation() was called\\n- mDefaultPrevented: preventDefault() was called\\n\\nListeners can be configured as:\\n- Capturing (capture=true) - fires in capture phase\\n- Bubbling (capture=false) - fires in bubble phase and target phase\\n- Passive - cannot call preventDefault()\\n- Once - automatically removed after first invocation\\n\\n## 7. Shadow DOM and Retargeting\\n\\nThe event system handles:\\n- Event retargeting across shadow boundaries (EventChainPreVisitor lines 137-140)\\n- Composed path calculation considering shadow trees\\n- Target adjustment based on shadow tree composition\\n- Anonymous content retargeting\\n\\n## 8. Key Data Structures\\n\\n**EventChainVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:53-111)\\n- Base visitor for event chain traversal\\n- Contains: presContext, event, mDOMEvent, eventStatus, itemFlags, itemData\\n\\n**EventChainPreVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:113-260)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor with pre-dispatch state\\n- Tracks: canHandle, automaticChromeDispatch, retargeted targets, parent targets\\n\\n**EventChainPostVisitor** (EventDispatcher.h:318-330)\\n- Extends EventChainVisitor for post-dispatch operations\\n- Used after event listener invocation\\n- Carries PostHandleEvent results\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe complete event dispatch flow is:\\n\\n1. EventTarget::DispatchEvent \u2192 EventDispatcher::Dispatch (creates chain)\\n2. Build event target chain via GetEventTargetParent (up to document/window)\\n3. Call PreHandleEvent on all targets (setup phase)\\n4. HandleEventTargetChain iterates:\\n   - Capture phase: root \u2192 target, invoke capture listeners\\n   - Target phase: invoke all listeners on original target\\n   - Bubble phase: target \u2192 root, invoke bubble listeners\\n5. PostHandleEvent called after listeners (post-processing)\\n6. Default group dispatch completes\\n7. System group dispatch with same phases\\n8. ActivationBehavior executed if not prevented (default action)\\n\\nThis design separates concerns between event routing, listener management, and default action handling, allowing flexible event processing in Firefox's DOM implementation.\"\n}\n",
